name:F‚Äçe‚Äçi‚Äçy‚Äçi‚Äçb‚Äça‚Äçn‚Äçg‚Äça‚Äçn‚Äçs‚Äçh‚Äço‚Äçu

posted:Posted July 4, 2021
msg:Zero points, the reason is: discrimination + fraud.

Xinglin Bay Hotel discriminates against Internet channel guests (such as Ctrip). Swimming and other facilities charge Internet channel guests, but it is free for front desk guests. For online users booking, please be sure to understand the service content and record in advance. Details are as follows:

On business trips in Xiamen, I often choose to stay at Xinglinwan Hotel. I should have stayed for 9 nights this year. Not many tourists or business travelers live here. After all, the main focus of the hotel is "away from the city" and "conference hotel." It attracts me the most, that is: swimming. I can enjoy swimming facilities every time in the past.

But today, I must say goodbye and give this hotel zero points. Because, this time I stayed, the hotel suddenly said that swimming is not provided. If you want to swim, it costs 158 yuan per trip (I thought it was the personal behavior of the hotel staff). The explanation of the hotel account manager is:
1. The price is low for guests who book through Ctrip.com, and there is no free swimming service. According to the internal notice of the hotel, since 71, online booking customers will no longer send it. Only guests staying on site can swim for free. However, this difference is not indicated on the Internet.
Second, the facilities and services on Ctrip's website indicate swimming, but it does not indicate free. The webpage is only an introduction to the service content, and does not mean that it is provided for free. Indeed, the free parking is clearly written, and the others neither say free nor charge. I seem to be unable to refute this, but if the hotel on Ctrip charges a swimming pool, it will usually be clearly stated.
Third, I came to live before and can swim. That is a gift, and it doesn't mean I will give it away in the future. (It seems that what I used to be a charity, not a service, I am a bit self-righteous.)

So, my understanding is:
1. The free facilities are marked on the webpage and the hotel can provide them. Free facilities are not marked, the hotel provides them depending on the mood. If you are an internet channel, the hotel may be in a bad mood. The price is low, it seems that he is not setting the price online. The hotel does not think it needs to make special instructions on the internet for the adjus**ent and change of these service charges.
Second, low Internet prices are just a means of soliciting customers. You think it is affordable. When you come to this remote place, it is not appropriate to spend time and take a taxi to change hotels. If you want to enjoy the facilities, then pay for it. You think that the services on the page are included in the room rate, then you are fooled. I don‚Äôt know what other services are chargeable except for swimming. I hope that Xinglinwan Hotel is not the Xuexiang of slaughter.
Third, it used to be free, but now it is charged. There is no need to clearly inform the webpage. The hotel thinks it is legal and compliant, but obviously this is also his trick to cheat customers.
Fourth, online and offline customers from different sources are treated differently, which discriminates against online booking customers. It is strange that there are still businesses that do this business, and everyone is trying to develop customers through online channels. Don't play if you can't afford it, don't fool people with low online prices. I guess he is a state-owned enterprise. But I think there is a big problem with five-star hotels making this distinction.
Fifth, in fact, this is not just discrimination, it is fraud. On the Ctrip APP, the hotel manager‚Äôs official reply to the guests is clear: the swimming pool can be used for free. As shown in the figure. This is the hotel‚Äôs response five months after the guest‚Äôs question.
Sixth, communicate with the lobby manager, the lobby manager does not quarrel or scold, but does not solve the problem. But the lobby manager also made it clear: this kind of customer's problem, the highest point is his, the hotel has no other channels to solve it. His solution was to explain to me verbally that he had to pay for it if he really wanted to swim. Hehe, in my opinion, this kind of trea**ent is the arrogance of the hotel.

Maybe a customer like me is not an old customer, so it doesn't matter. The above content is recorded. This kind of hotel, I do not hope that he can respond to me. But I hope that the online platform can explain it. Your business is too bad. It provides inferior services to online customers. It is necessary for the platform to regulate it.
